 Let's know what is the importance of Shivling and its glory
 
 
 shivlinga kii mahima-- shivlinga ko shiv ji kaa niraakaar swaroop mana jaataa he
 - It is most recognized in Shiva worship
 - shivlinga main shiv or shakti donon hi samahit hote hai
 - Worshiping both of them becomes complete by worshiping Shivalinga
 - poojane ke liye alag-alag prakaar ke shivlinga prachlit hai
 - Among them are Swayambhu Shivling, Narmadeshwar Shivling, Janaudhari Shivling, gold-silver Shivling and Parad Shivling
 - swayambhu shivlinga kii puja sabase zyada mahatvapurn or faldaayi maani jaati he
 - Rules of establishment of Shivling - worship of Shivling is most important in Shiva worship
 - shivlinga ghar main alag or mandir main alag tareeke se sthapit hota he
 - The altar of Shivalinga should be facing towards north
 - ghar main sthapit shivlinga bahut zyada bada nahin hona chahie
 - The Shivling installed in the house should be more than 6 inches
 - mandir main kitna bhi bada shivlinga sthapit kar sakate hai
 - For special wishes, worshiping is done by setting up the mortal Shivling
 bholenath ko prasann karne ke liye shivlinga kii upasna hi sabase adbhut he
 But apart from the glory of Shivalinga and the rule of offering dear things to Lord Shiva on it, there is also a special mantra
 shivlinga par kuch bhi arpit karte samay is vishesh mantra kaa jaap karnaa shubh faldaayak mana jaataa he
 This is the special mantra - While offering any substance on Shivling, chant this special mantra - 'om Namah Shambhavai Ch, Mayobhavaya Ch, Namah Shankarai Ch, Mayskarai Ch, Namah Shivaya Ch, Shivatarai Ch' punjab ke up-mukhyamantri sukhbir singh badal ko faridakot kii ek adaalat ne chunaav ke dauraan hinsa karne ke maamle main bari kar diya

 How to check lost and milk sitting at home
 
 
 - synthetic doodh, maave or khoe se bani mithai main mukhya rup se do chizon kii milawat hoti he
 In the lost starch, the same amount of urea to increase the protein content of milk, and both are harmful for our health
 - storch or uria kii jaanch ke liye aapako chahie thodaa sa iodine solution jo ki kisi bhi chemist shop main aasaani se mil jayega
 Apart from this, you need Paradimethyl Amino Benzaldehyde, its solution will also be found in the Chemical Shop
 - doodh paneer yaa khoe kii mithai main storch he yaa nahin ye jaanane ke liye ek kaanch ke boul main thode se paneer yaa mithai ko gunagune pani main puri tarah ghulne den
 When paneer and khoya sweets are completely dissolved in water, add four to five drops of iodine solution to it, do the same process with milk
 - iodine milaane ke baad agar doodh, paneer yaa khoe kii mithai ke solution kaa rang nila ho jaae to samajhie ye milavati he
 - And if the color of this mixture does not change, it means that it is pure
 - uria aksar synthetic doodh main milaayaa jaataa he or us doodh se bane paneer yaa khoe main bhi mil jaataa he
 To test it, make a mixture of cottage cheese or khoya in hot water as before, and add a few drops of Paradimethyl amino benzaldehyde to it - if there is a quantity of urea in it, the color will turn yellow
